

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Tahoe/RCMP_Unmarked_Tahoe/Config/TDPatterns/LeftRight.lua ---

--[[
    LeftRight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Tahoe → RCMP Unmarked Tahoe → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R2 = tdModule(ELSModel.R2);

	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(1);
			R3(1);
			R6(1);
			R7(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			wait(0.3);
			R2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			wait(0.2);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		R7(1);
		R6(1);
		R5(1);
		R4(1);
		R3(1);
		R2(1);
	end
end


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Tahoe/RCMP_Unmarked_Tahoe/Config/TDPatterns/Line.lua ---

--[[
    Line (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Tahoe → RCMP Unmarked Tahoe → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R2 = tdModule(ELSModel.R2);

	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			wait(0.3);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		R7(1);
		R6(1);
		R5(1);
		R4(1);
		R3(1);
		R2(1);
	end
end


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Tahoe/RCMP_Unmarked_Tahoe/Config/TDPatterns/Right.lua ---

--[[
    Right (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Tahoe → RCMP Unmarked Tahoe → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R2 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R2);

	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			wait(0.2);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		R7(1);
		R6(1);
		R5(1);
		R4(1);
		R3(1);
		R2(1);
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Grey_Taurus/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Grey Taurus → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);
return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1);
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2);

	local G1 = elsModule(ELSModel.G1);
	local G2 = elsModule(ELSModel.G2);

	local X1 = elsModule(ELSModel.X1);
	local X2 = elsModule(ELSModel.X2);


	local H1 = elsModule(ELSModel.H1);
	local H2 = elsModule(ELSModel.H2);
	
	local M1 = elsModule(ELSModel.M1);
	local M2 = elsModule(ELSModel.M2);
	
	local S1 = elsModule(ELSModel.S1);
	local S2 = elsModule(ELSModel.S2);
	
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1);
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2);
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R5 = elsModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R6 = elsModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R7 = elsModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R8 = elsModule(ELSModel.R8);
	if enabled then
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					F1(1);
					F2(1);
					wait(0)
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					G1(0);
					G2(1);
					wait(0.07)
					G1(1);
					G2(1);
					wait(0.07)
					G1(0);
					G2(1);
					wait(0.07)
					G1(1);
					G2(1);
					wait(0.07)
					G1(0);
					G2(1);
					wait(0.4)
					G1(1);
					G2(0);
					wait(0.07)
					G1(1);
					G2(1);
					wait(0.07)
					G1(1);
					G2(0);
					wait(0.07)
					G1(1);
					G2(1);
					wait(0.07)
					G1(1);
					G2(0);
					wait(0.4)
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					H1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));
					H2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));
					wait(00)
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					X1(1);
					X2(0);
					wait(0.06)
					X1(1);
					X2(1);
					wait(0.06)
					X1(1);
					X2(0);
					wait(0.06)
					X1(1);
					X2(1);
					wait(0.06)
					X1(1);
					X2(0);
					wait(0.06)
					X1(1);
					X2(1);
					wait(0.06)
					X1(1);
					X2(0);
					wait(0.06)
					X1(1);
					X2(1);
					wait(0.06)
					X1(0);
					X2(1);
					wait(0.06)
					X1(1);
					X2(1);
					wait(0.06)
					X1(0);
					X2(1);
					wait(0.06)
					X1(1);
					X2(1);
					wait(0.06)
					X1(0);
					X2(1);
					wait(0.06)
					X1(1);
					X2(1);
					wait(0.06)
					X1(0);
					X2(1);
					wait(0.06)
					X1(1);
					X2(1);
					wait(0.06)
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					M1(1);
					M2(1);
					wait(0)
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					S1(1);
					S2(1);
					wait(0)
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					R2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
					R3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
					R4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
					R5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
					R6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
					R7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
					wait(0)
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					R1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R8(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					wait(0)
				end
			end)
		end)
	else
		G1(1);
		G2(1);	
		F1(1);
		F2(1);
		X1(1);
		X2(1);	
		H1(1);
		H2(1);
		R1(1);
		R2(1);
		R3(1);
		R4(1);
		R5(1);
		R6(1);
		R7(1);
		R8(1);
		M1(1);
		M2(1);
		S1(1);
		S2(1);
	end
end

	local X2 = elsModule(ELSModel.X2);

	local H1 = elsModule(ELSModel.H1);
	local H2 = elsModule(ELSModel.H2);
	
	local M1 = elsModule(ELSModel.M1);
	local M2 = elsModule(ELSModel.M2);

	local S2 = elsModule(ELSModel.S2);

	if enabled then
		task.spawn(function()

					wait(0.7)
				end
			end)

			pcall(function()
				while true do
					R2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
					R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
					R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
					R5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Grey_Taurus/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Grey Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Grey_Taurus/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Grey Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Grey_Taurus/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Grey Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Grey_Taurus/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Grey Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Grey_Taurus/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

    Reverselights (ModuleScript)

    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));

			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);

			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Slicktop_Taurus/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Slicktop Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Slicktop_Taurus/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Slicktop Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Slicktop_Taurus/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Slicktop Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Slicktop_Taurus/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Slicktop Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Slicktop_Taurus/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Slicktop Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47

local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Slicktop_Taurus/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Slicktop Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Slicktop_Taurus/Config/TDPatterns/Left.lua ---

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Slicktop Taurus → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R2 = tdModule(ELSModel.R2);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Taurus/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Taurus/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Taurus/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Taurus/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Taurus/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Taurus/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Taurus/Config/Modules/TdPart.lua ---

--[[
    TdPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Unmarked_Taurus/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Unmarked Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Unmarked_Taurus/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Unmarked Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Unmarked_Taurus/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Unmarked Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Unmarked_Taurus/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Unmarked Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Unmarked_Taurus/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Unmarked Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Royal_Canadian_Mounted_Police/RCMP_Taurus/RCMP_Unmarked_Taurus/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Royal Canadian Mounted Police → RCMP Taurus → RCMP Unmarked Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R2 = tdModule(ELSModel.R2);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			wait(0.2);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_FL-70_Salter/Body/SnowPlow/Plow/Detection/PlowServer.server.lua ---

--[[
    PlowServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL FL-70 Salter → Body → SnowPlow → Plow → Detection
    Parent: Detection
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local mathAbs = math.abs;
local newVector3 = Vector3.new;
local newRegion3 = Region3.new;

function PartToRegion3(part)
	local cf = part.CFrame;
	local size = part.Size;
	local sx, sy, sz = size.X, size.Y, size.Z;

	local x, y, z, R00, R01, R02, R10, R11, R12, R20, R21, R22 = cf:components();

	local wsx = 0.5 * (mathAbs(R00) * sx + mathAbs(R01) * sy + mathAbs(R02) * sz);
	local wsy = 0.5 * (mathAbs(R10) * sx + mathAbs(R11) * sy + mathAbs(R12) * sz);
	local wsz = 0.5 * (mathAbs(R20) * sx + mathAbs(R21) * sy + mathAbs(R22) * sz);

	local minx = x - wsx;
	local miny = y - wsy;
	local minz = z - wsz;

	local maxx = x + wsx;
	local maxy = y + wsy;
	local maxz = z + wsz;

	local minv, maxv = newVector3(minx, miny, minz), newVector3(maxx, maxy, maxz);

	return newRegion3(minv, maxv);
end;

while true do
	--local ray = Ray.new(script.Parent.Position, Vector3.new(0, 0, 10));
	--local hit, hitPos, normal, material = workspace:FindPartOnRay(ray, nil, nil, true);
	--print(hit, material);
	--if material == Enum.Material.Sand and hit:IsA('Terrain') then
	workspace.Terrain:ReplaceMaterial(PartToRegion3(script.Parent), 4, Enum.Material.Sand, Enum.Material.Air);
	--end;
	task.wait(0.25)
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_FL-70_Salter/Body/SnowPlow/PlowWeldServer.server.lua ---

--[[
    PlowWeldServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL FL-70 Salter → Body → SnowPlow
    Parent: SnowPlow
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
local PlowModel = script.Parent.Plow;
local Stick = script.Parent.Stick;

local Vertical = Stick.Vertical;
local Horizontal = Stick.Horizontal;

local Main = script.Parent.Main; --Acts like platform part

local function WeldParts(part0: BasePart, part1: BasePart, name: string?): Weld
	local weld = Instance.new('Weld');
	weld.Parent = part0;
	weld.Part0 = part0;
	weld.Part1 = part1;
	weld.Parent = part0;
	weld.Name = name or 'Weld' 
	weld.C1 = part1.CFrame:Inverse() * part0.CFrame;
	return weld;
end

for _,v in next, Horizontal:GetChildren() do
	if v ~= Horizontal.BallConnect or v ~= Horizontal.Ball then
		local weld = WeldParts(Horizontal.Ball, v);
	end;
end;

local horizontalWeld = WeldParts(Horizontal.Joint, Horizontal.Ball, 'ConnectingJoint');
local verticalWeld = WeldParts(Vertical.Ball, Horizontal.Ball, 'PivotConnection');

for _,v in next, Vertical:GetChildren() do
	if v ~= Vertical.Ball then
		WeldParts(Vertical.Ball, v);
	end;
end;

for _,v in next, PlowModel:GetDescendants() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') then
		WeldParts(Vertical.Ball,  v);
	end;
end;

for _,v in next, script.Parent:GetChildren() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') then
		WeldParts(Main, v);
	end;
end;

for _,v in next, script.Parent.LightFrame:GetDescendants() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') then
		WeldParts(Main, v);
	end;
end

horizontalWeld:SetAttribute('Centre', horizontalWeld.C0);
horizontalWeld:SetAttribute('Right', horizontalWeld.C0 * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(30), 0, 0));
horizontalWeld:SetAttribute('Left', horizontalWeld.C0 * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-30), 0, 0));

verticalWeld:SetAttribute('Down', verticalWeld.C0);
verticalWeld:SetAttribute('Up', verticalWeld.C0 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.rad(-45)))

script.Parent.Parent.Parent.CarServer.Enabled = true;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_FL-70_Salter/CarServer.server.lua ---

--[[
    CarServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL FL-70 Salter
    Parent: TL FL-70 Salter
    Properties:
        Disabled: true
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
--[[local Knit = require(game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Knit);

Knit.OnStart():await();

require(Knit.Modules.Car).new(script.Parent, false);]]

game:GetService('ServerScriptService'):WaitForChild('AeroLoaded');

_G.Aero.Modules.Car.new(script.Parent, true);

local vehicleSeat = script.Parent.Chassis.VehicleSeat;

local lastPlayer;

vehicleSeat:GetAttributeChangedSignal('LastOccupant'):Connect(function()
	local occupant = vehicleSeat:GetAttribute('LastOccupant');

	if occupant ~= nil then
		local player = game.Players:FindFirstChild(occupant);
		if player then
			if player.Team.Name == 'Translink' then
				lastPlayer = player;
				_G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.Send(player, 'SnowPlowGuiVisibility', true);
			end
		end;
	elseif occupant == nil and lastPlayer then
		if lastPlayer:IsDescendantOf(game.Players) then
			_G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.Send(lastPlayer, 'SnowPlowGuiVisibility', false);
		else
			lastPlayer = nil;
		end
	end;
end);


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_FL-70_Salter/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL FL-70 Salter → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:47
]]
return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	if enabled then
		local rotLights = ELSModel.RotLights;
		for i, v in next, rotLights:GetChildren() do
			v.Light.SpotLight.Enabled = true;
		end;
		while true do
			for i = 1, 360, 15 do
				for i2, v in next, rotLights:GetChildren() do
					local orientation = Vector3.new(0, v.OppositeDirection.Value and -i or i, 0);
					v.Chrome.Orientation = orientation;
					v.Light.Orientation = orientation;
				end;
				wait();
			end;
			wait();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, ELSModel.RotLights:GetChildren() do
			v.Light.SpotLight.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do

		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do

			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_FL-70_Salter/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL FL-70 Salter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;
	
	local frontLights = headlights.Front;

	if enabled then
		
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
		end;
		
		for _,v in next, frontLights:GetChildren() do
			if v:IsA('Beam') or v:IsA('SpotLight') then
				v.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
		
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
		end;

		for _,v in next, headlights.Front:GetChildren() do
			if v:IsA('Beam') or v:IsA('SpotLight') then
				v.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_FL-70_Salter/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL FL-70 Salter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_FL-70_Salter/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL FL-70 Salter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48

local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_FL-70_Salter/Config/Modules/TdPart.lua ---

--[[
    TdPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL FL-70 Salter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_FL-70_Salter_Orange/Body/SnowPlow/Plow/Detection/PlowServer.server.lua ---

--[[
    PlowServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL FL-70 Salter Orange → Body → SnowPlow → Plow → Detection
    Parent: Detection
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local mathAbs = math.abs;
local newVector3 = Vector3.new;
local newRegion3 = Region3.new;

function PartToRegion3(part)
	local cf = part.CFrame;
	local size = part.Size;
	local sx, sy, sz = size.X, size.Y, size.Z;

	local x, y, z, R00, R01, R02, R10, R11, R12, R20, R21, R22 = cf:components();

	local wsx = 0.5 * (mathAbs(R00) * sx + mathAbs(R01) * sy + mathAbs(R02) * sz);
	local wsy = 0.5 * (mathAbs(R10) * sx + mathAbs(R11) * sy + mathAbs(R12) * sz);
	local wsz = 0.5 * (mathAbs(R20) * sx + mathAbs(R21) * sy + mathAbs(R22) * sz);

	local minx = x - wsx;
	local miny = y - wsy;
	local minz = z - wsz;

	local maxx = x + wsx;
	local maxy = y + wsy;
	local maxz = z + wsz;

	local minv, maxv = newVector3(minx, miny, minz), newVector3(maxx, maxy, maxz);

	return newRegion3(minv, maxv);
end;

while true do
	--local ray = Ray.new(script.Parent.Position, Vector3.new(0, 0, 10));
	--local hit, hitPos, normal, material = workspace:FindPartOnRay(ray, nil, nil, true);
	--print(hit, material);
	--if material == Enum.Material.Sand and hit:IsA('Terrain') then
	workspace.Terrain:ReplaceMaterial(PartToRegion3(script.Parent), 4, Enum.Material.Sand, Enum.Material.Air);
	--end;
	task.wait(0.25)
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_FL-70_Salter_Orange/Body/SnowPlow/PlowWeldServer.server.lua ---

--[[
    PlowWeldServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL FL-70 Salter Orange → Body → SnowPlow
    Parent: SnowPlow
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local PlowModel = script.Parent.Plow;
local Stick = script.Parent.Stick;

local Vertical = Stick.Vertical;
local Horizontal = Stick.Horizontal;

local Main = script.Parent.Main; --Acts like platform part

local function WeldParts(part0: BasePart, part1: BasePart, name: string?): Weld
	local weld = Instance.new('Weld');
	weld.Parent = part0;
	weld.Part0 = part0;
	weld.Part1 = part1;
	weld.Parent = part0;
	weld.Name = name or 'Weld' 
	weld.C1 = part1.CFrame:Inverse() * part0.CFrame;
	return weld;
end

for _,v in next, Horizontal:GetChildren() do
	if v ~= Horizontal.BallConnect or v ~= Horizontal.Ball then
		local weld = WeldParts(Horizontal.Ball, v);
	end;
end;

local horizontalWeld = WeldParts(Horizontal.Joint, Horizontal.Ball, 'ConnectingJoint');
local verticalWeld = WeldParts(Vertical.Ball, Horizontal.Ball, 'PivotConnection');

for _,v in next, Vertical:GetChildren() do
	if v ~= Vertical.Ball then
		WeldParts(Vertical.Ball, v);
	end;
end;

for _,v in next, PlowModel:GetDescendants() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') then
		WeldParts(Vertical.Ball,  v);
	end;
end;

for _,v in next, script.Parent:GetChildren() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') then
		WeldParts(Main, v);
	end;
end;

for _,v in next, script.Parent.LightFrame:GetDescendants() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') then
		WeldParts(Main, v);
	end;
end

horizontalWeld:SetAttribute('Centre', horizontalWeld.C0);
horizontalWeld:SetAttribute('Right', horizontalWeld.C0 * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(30), 0, 0));
horizontalWeld:SetAttribute('Left', horizontalWeld.C0 * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-30), 0, 0));

verticalWeld:SetAttribute('Down', verticalWeld.C0);
verticalWeld:SetAttribute('Up', verticalWeld.C0 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.rad(-45)))

script.Parent.Parent.Parent.CarServer.Enabled = true;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_FL-70_Salter_Orange/CarServer.server.lua ---

--[[
    CarServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL FL-70 Salter Orange
    Parent: TL FL-70 Salter Orange
    Properties:
        Disabled: true
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
--[[local Knit = require(game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Knit);

Knit.OnStart():await();

require(Knit.Modules.Car).new(script.Parent, false);]]

game:GetService('ServerScriptService'):WaitForChild('AeroLoaded');

_G.Aero.Modules.Car.new(script.Parent, true);

local vehicleSeat = script.Parent.Chassis.VehicleSeat;

local lastPlayer;

vehicleSeat:GetAttributeChangedSignal('LastOccupant'):Connect(function()
	local occupant = vehicleSeat:GetAttribute('LastOccupant');

	if occupant ~= nil then
		local player = game.Players:FindFirstChild(occupant);
		if player then
			if player.Team.Name == 'Translink' then
				lastPlayer = player;
				_G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.Send(player, 'SnowPlowGuiVisibility', true);
			end
		end;
	elseif occupant == nil and lastPlayer then
		if lastPlayer:IsDescendantOf(game.Players) then
			_G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.Send(lastPlayer, 'SnowPlowGuiVisibility', false);
		else
			lastPlayer = nil;
		end
	end;
end);


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_FL-70_Salter_Orange/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL FL-70 Salter Orange → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	if enabled then
		local rotLights = ELSModel.RotLights;
		for i, v in next, rotLights:GetChildren() do
			v.Light.SpotLight.Enabled = true;
		end;
		while true do
			for i = 1, 360, 15 do
				for i2, v in next, rotLights:GetChildren() do
					local orientation = Vector3.new(0, v.OppositeDirection.Value and -i or i, 0);
					v.Chrome.Orientation = orientation;
					v.Light.Orientation = orientation;
				end;
				wait();
			end;
			wait();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, ELSModel.RotLights:GetChildren() do
			v.Light.SpotLight.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_FL-70_Salter_Orange/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL FL-70 Salter Orange → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_FL-70_Salter_Orange/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL FL-70 Salter Orange → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;
	
	local frontLights = headlights.Front;

	if enabled then
		
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
		end;
		
		for _,v in next, frontLights:GetChildren() do
			if v:IsA('Beam') or v:IsA('SpotLight') then
				v.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
		
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
		end;

		for _,v in next, headlights.Front:GetChildren() do
			if v:IsA('Beam') or v:IsA('SpotLight') then
				v.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_FL-70_Salter_Orange/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL FL-70 Salter Orange → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_FL-70_Salter_Orange/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL FL-70 Salter Orange → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_FL-70_Salter_Orange/Config/Modules/TdPart.lua ---

--[[
    TdPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL FL-70 Salter Orange → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_Salter_F-350/Body/SnowPlow/Plow/Detection/PlowServer.server.lua ---

--[[
    PlowServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL Salter F-350 → Body → SnowPlow → Plow → Detection
    Parent: Detection
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local mathAbs = math.abs;
local newVector3 = Vector3.new;
local newRegion3 = Region3.new;

function PartToRegion3(part)
	local cf = part.CFrame;
	local size = part.Size;
	local sx, sy, sz = size.X, size.Y, size.Z;

	local x, y, z, R00, R01, R02, R10, R11, R12, R20, R21, R22 = cf:components();

	local wsx = 0.5 * (mathAbs(R00) * sx + mathAbs(R01) * sy + mathAbs(R02) * sz);
	local wsy = 0.5 * (mathAbs(R10) * sx + mathAbs(R11) * sy + mathAbs(R12) * sz);
	local wsz = 0.5 * (mathAbs(R20) * sx + mathAbs(R21) * sy + mathAbs(R22) * sz);

	local minx = x - wsx;
	local miny = y - wsy;
	local minz = z - wsz;

	local maxx = x + wsx;
	local maxy = y + wsy;
	local maxz = z + wsz;

	local minv, maxv = newVector3(minx, miny, minz), newVector3(maxx, maxy, maxz);

	return newRegion3(minv, maxv);
end;

while true do
	--local ray = Ray.new(script.Parent.Position, Vector3.new(0, 0, 10));
	--local hit, hitPos, normal, material = workspace:FindPartOnRay(ray, nil, nil, true);
	--print(hit, material);
	--if material == Enum.Material.Sand and hit:IsA('Terrain') then
	workspace.Terrain:ReplaceMaterial(PartToRegion3(script.Parent), 4, Enum.Material.Sand, Enum.Material.Air);
	--end;
	task.wait(0.25)
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_Salter_F-350/Body/SnowPlow/PlowWeldServer.server.lua ---

--[[
    PlowWeldServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL Salter F-350 → Body → SnowPlow
    Parent: SnowPlow
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local PlowModel = script.Parent.Plow;
local Stick = script.Parent.Stick;

local Vertical = Stick.Vertical;
local Horizontal = Stick.Horizontal;

local Main = script.Parent.Main; --Acts like platform part

local function WeldParts(part0: BasePart, part1: BasePart, name: string?): Weld
	local weld = Instance.new('Weld');
	weld.Parent = part0;
	weld.Part0 = part0;
	weld.Part1 = part1;
	weld.Parent = part0;
	weld.Name = name or 'Weld' 
	weld.C1 = part1.CFrame:Inverse() * part0.CFrame;
	return weld;
end

for _,v in next, Horizontal:GetChildren() do
	if v ~= Horizontal.BallConnect or v ~= Horizontal.Ball then
		local weld = WeldParts(Horizontal.Ball, v);
	end;
end;

local horizontalWeld = WeldParts(Horizontal.Joint, Horizontal.Ball, 'ConnectingJoint');
local verticalWeld = WeldParts(Vertical.Ball, Horizontal.Ball, 'PivotConnection');

for _,v in next, Vertical:GetChildren() do
	if v ~= Vertical.Ball then
		WeldParts(Vertical.Ball, v);
	end;
end;

for _,v in next, PlowModel:GetDescendants() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') then
		WeldParts(Vertical.Ball,  v);
	end;
end;

for _,v in next, script.Parent:GetChildren() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') then
		WeldParts(Main, v);
	end;
end;

for _,v in next, script.Parent.LightFrame:GetDescendants() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') then
		WeldParts(Main, v);
	end;
end

horizontalWeld:SetAttribute('Centre', horizontalWeld.C0);
horizontalWeld:SetAttribute('Right', horizontalWeld.C0 * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(30), 0, 0));
horizontalWeld:SetAttribute('Left', horizontalWeld.C0 * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-30), 0, 0));

verticalWeld:SetAttribute('Down', verticalWeld.C0);
verticalWeld:SetAttribute('Up', verticalWeld.C0 * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.rad(-45)))

script.Parent.Parent.Parent.CarServer.Enabled = true;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_Salter_F-350/CarServer.server.lua ---

--[[
    CarServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL Salter F-350
    Parent: TL Salter F-350
    Properties:
        Disabled: true
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
--[[local Knit = require(game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Knit);

Knit.OnStart():await();

require(Knit.Modules.Car).new(script.Parent, false);]]

game:GetService('ServerScriptService'):WaitForChild('AeroLoaded');

_G.Aero.Modules.Car.new(script.Parent, true);

local vehicleSeat = script.Parent.Chassis.VehicleSeat;

local lastPlayer;

vehicleSeat:GetAttributeChangedSignal('LastOccupant'):Connect(function()
	local occupant = vehicleSeat:GetAttribute('LastOccupant');

	if occupant ~= nil then
		local player = game.Players:FindFirstChild(occupant);
		if player then
			if player.Team.Name == 'Translink' then
				lastPlayer = player;
				_G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.Send(player, 'SnowPlowGuiVisibility', true);
			end
		end;
	elseif occupant == nil and lastPlayer then
		if lastPlayer:IsDescendantOf(game.Players) then
			_G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.Send(lastPlayer, 'SnowPlowGuiVisibility', false);
		else
			lastPlayer = nil;
		end
	end;
end);

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_Salter_F-350/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL Salter F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_Salter_F-350/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL Salter F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_Salter_F-350/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL Salter F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_Salter_F-350/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL Salter F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				if v:FindFirstChild('Attachment') then
					v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = true;
				else
					v.Light.Enabled = true;
				end
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				if v:FindFirstChild('Attachment') then
					v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = false;
				else
					v.Light.Enabled = false;
				end
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			if v:FindFirstChild('Attachment') then
				v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = false;
			else
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_Salter_F-350/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL Salter F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_Snow_Plow_F-350/Body/SnowPlow/Plow/Detection/PlowServer.server.lua ---

--[[
    PlowServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL Snow Plow F-350 → Body → SnowPlow → Plow → Detection
    Parent: Detection
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local mathAbs = math.abs;
local newVector3 = Vector3.new;
local newRegion3 = Region3.new;

function PartToRegion3(part)
	local cf = part.CFrame;
	local size = part.Size;
	local sx, sy, sz = size.X, size.Y, size.Z;

	local x, y, z, R00, R01, R02, R10, R11, R12, R20, R21, R22 = cf:components();

	local wsx = 0.5 * (mathAbs(R00) * sx + mathAbs(R01) * sy + mathAbs(R02) * sz);
	local wsy = 0.5 * (mathAbs(R10) * sx + mathAbs(R11) * sy + mathAbs(R12) * sz);
	local wsz = 0.5 * (mathAbs(R20) * sx + mathAbs(R21) * sy + mathAbs(R22) * sz);

	local minx = x - wsx;
	local miny = y - wsy;
	local minz = z - wsz;

	local maxx = x + wsx;
	local maxy = y + wsy;
	local maxz = z + wsz;

	local minv, maxv = newVector3(minx, miny, minz), newVector3(maxx, maxy, maxz);

	return newRegion3(minv, maxv);
end;

while true do
	--local ray = Ray.new(script.Parent.Position, Vector3.new(0, 0, 10));
	--local hit, hitPos, normal, material = workspace:FindPartOnRay(ray, nil, nil, true);
	--print(hit, material);
	--if material == Enum.Material.Sand and hit:IsA('Terrain') then
	workspace.Terrain:ReplaceMaterial(PartToRegion3(script.Parent), 4, Enum.Material.Sand, Enum.Material.Air);
	--end;
	task.wait(0.25)
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_Snow_Plow_F-350/Body/SnowPlow/PlowWeldServer.server.lua ---

--[[
    PlowWeldServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL Snow Plow F-350 → Body → SnowPlow
    Parent: SnowPlow
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local PlowModel = script.Parent.Plow;
local Stick = script.Parent.Stick;

local Vertical = Stick.Vertical;
local Horizontal = Stick.Horizontal;

local Main = script.Parent.Main; --Acts like platform part

local function WeldParts(part0: BasePart, part1: BasePart, name: string?): Weld
	local weld = Instance.new('Weld');
	weld.Parent = part0;
	weld.Part0 = part0;
	weld.Part1 = part1;
	weld.Parent = part0;
	weld.Name = name or 'Weld' 
	weld.C1 = part1.CFrame:Inverse() * part0.CFrame;
	return weld;
end

for _,v in next, Horizontal:GetChildren() do
	if v ~= Horizontal.BallConnect or v ~= Horizontal.Ball then
		local weld = WeldParts(Horizontal.Ball, v);
	end;
end;

local horizontalWeld = WeldParts(Horizontal.Joint, Horizontal.Ball, 'ConnectingJoint');
local verticalWeld = WeldParts(Vertical.Ball, Horizontal.Ball, 'PivotConnection');

for _,v in next, Vertical:GetChildren() do
	if v ~= Vertical.Ball then
		WeldParts(Vertical.Ball, v);
	end;
end;

for _,v in next, PlowModel:GetDescendants() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') then
		WeldParts(Vertical.Ball,  v);
	end;
end;

for _,v in next, script.Parent:GetChildren() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') then
		WeldParts(Main, v);
	end;
end;

for _,v in next, script.Parent.LightFrame:GetDescendants() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') then
		WeldParts(Main, v);
	end;
end

horizontalWeld:SetAttribute('Centre', horizontalWeld.C0);

--[[local Knit = require(game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').Knit);

game:GetService('ServerScriptService'):WaitForChild('AeroLoaded');

_G.Aero.Modules.Car.new(script.Parent, true);

local vehicleSeat = script.Parent.Chassis.VehicleSeat;

local lastPlayer;

vehicleSeat:GetAttributeChangedSignal('LastOccupant'):Connect(function()
	local occupant = vehicleSeat:GetAttribute('LastOccupant');

	if occupant ~= nil then
		local player = game.Players:FindFirstChild(occupant);
		if player then
			if player.Team.Name == 'Translink' then
				lastPlayer = player;
				_G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.Send(player, 'SnowPlowGuiVisibility', true);
			end
		end;
	elseif occupant == nil and lastPlayer then
		if lastPlayer:IsDescendantOf(game.Players) then
			_G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.Send(lastPlayer, 'SnowPlowGuiVisibility', false);
		else
			lastPlayer = nil;
		end
	end;
end);
