================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_Snow_Plow_F-350/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL Snow Plow F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_Snow_Plow_F-350/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL Snow Plow F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_Snow_Plow_F-350/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL Snow Plow F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_Snow_Plow_F-350/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL Snow Plow F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				if v:FindFirstChild('Attachment') then
					v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = true;
				else
					v.Light.Enabled = true;
				end
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				if v:FindFirstChild('Attachment') then
					v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = false;
				else
					v.Light.Enabled = false;
				end
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			if v:FindFirstChild('Attachment') then
				v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = false;
			else
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/SO_Snow/TL_Snow_Plow_F-350/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → SO: Snow → TL Snow Plow F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/SO_F-150/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → SO F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/SO_F-150/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → SO F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/SO_F-150/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → SO F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/SO_F-150/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → SO F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/SO_F-150/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → SO F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/TA_Arrowboard_F-150/Body/Bed/weldBedServer.server.lua ---

--[[
    weldBedServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TA Arrowboard F-150 → Body → Bed
    Parent: Bed
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local platform = script.Parent.Parent.Parent.Chassis.Platform;
local platformCFrame = platform.CFrame;

local pivot = script.Parent.Pivot_1;
local pivotCFrame = pivot.CFrame;

local main = script.Parent.Pivot;
local mainCFrame = main.CFrame;

local board = script.Parent.Main;
local boardCFrame = board.CFrame;

local newInstance = Instance.new;

local descendants = script.Parent:GetDescendants();
for i = 1, #descendants do
	local v = descendants[i];
	if v:IsA('BasePart') and v ~= main and v.Name ~= 'Pivot_1' and v.Name ~= 'Main' then
		local w = newInstance('Weld');
		w.Part0 = board;
		w.Part1 = v;
		w.C1 = v.CFrame:Inverse() * boardCFrame;
		w.Parent = board;
		v.Anchored = false;
	end;
end;

local boardWeld = newInstance('Weld');
boardWeld.Name = 'BoardWeld';
boardWeld.Part0 = board;
boardWeld.Part1 = pivot;
boardWeld.C1 = pivotCFrame:Inverse() * boardCFrame;
boardWeld.Parent = board;
script.Parent.Main.Anchored = false;

local w = newInstance('Weld');
w.Name = 'BoardWeld';
w.Part0 = platform;
w.Part1 = main;
w.C1 = mainCFrame:Inverse() * platformCFrame;
w.Parent = platform;
main.Anchored = false;

					T4(1);
					wait(0.05);

					wait(0.12);

					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					wait(0.12);

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					wait(0.05);					

					R1(0);
					R2(0);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					wait(0.12);

					R1(1);
					R2(1);

					R4(1);
					wait(0.05);

					R2(1);

					R4(0);
					wait(0.12);

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					wait(0.05);							

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(0);
					R4(0);
					wait(0.12);

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					wait(0.05);										
				end
			end)
		end)()		

		coroutine.wrap(function()

					Q1(0);

					wait(0.12);

					Q1(1);
					Q2(1);
					wait(0.05);					

					Q1(0);

					Q1(1);
					Q2(1);
					wait(0.05);						
				end
			end)
		end)()		


	else
		T1(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
		T2(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/TA_Arrowboard_F-150/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TA Arrowboard F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/TA_Arrowboard_F-150/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TA Arrowboard F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/TA_Arrowboard_F-150/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TA Arrowboard F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/TA_Arrowboard_F-150/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TA Arrowboard F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/TA_Arrowboard_F-150/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TA Arrowboard F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Translink/Street_Ops/TA_Arrowboard_F-150/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TA Arrowboard F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

--[[
    Line (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Translink → Street Ops → TA Arrowboard F-150 → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:48
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local C1 = tdModule(ELSModel.C1);
	local L1 = tdModule(ELSModel.L1);
	local L2 = tdModule(ELSModel.L2);
	local L3 = tdModule(ELSModel.L3);
	local I3 = tdModule(ELSModel.I3);
	local I2 = tdModule(ELSModel.I2);
	local I1 = tdModule(ELSModel.I1);

	if enabled then
		ELSModel.C1:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.L1:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.L2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.L3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.I3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.I2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.I1:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			C1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L3(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L2(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I3(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I2(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			wait(0.2);
			C1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L3(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I3(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			wait(0.2);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.C1:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.L1:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.L2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.L3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.I3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.I2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.I1:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		C1(1);
		L3(1);
		L2(1);
		L1(1);
		I3(1);
		I2(1);
		I1(1);
	end
end

			I2(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I3(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			C1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L2(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L3(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RD1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RD2(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RU1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RU2(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			wait(0.2);
			I1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I3(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			C1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L3(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RD1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RD2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RU1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RU2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			wait(0.2);
			I1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I2(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I3(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			C1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L2(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L3(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RD1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RD2(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RU1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RU2(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			wait(0.2);
			I1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I3(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			C1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L3(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RD1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RD2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RU1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RU2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			wait(0.2);
			I1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I2(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I3(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			C1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L2(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L3(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RD1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RD2(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RU1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RU2(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			wait(0.2);
			I1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I3(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			C1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			L3(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RD1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RD2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RU1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			RU2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			wait(0.2);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.C1:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.I1:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.I2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.I3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.L1:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.L2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.L3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.RD1:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.RD2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.RU1:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.RU2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		C1(1);
		I3(1);
		I2(1);
		I1(1);
		L3(1);
		L2(1);
		L1(1);
		RD1(1);
		RD2(1);
		RU1(1);
		RU2(1);
	end
end
